***померанец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нец</a> (21742)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomeránec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померанец.html>помера́нцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bitter orange, wild orange</li>
<li>wild orange tree, bigarade</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:померещиться.html>помере́щиться</a> (17640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерещиться.html>мере́щиться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">meréščitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:померкнуть.html>поме́ркнуть</a> (14923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mérknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померкнуть.html>поме́ркнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomérknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow dark/dim</li>
<li>to fade, to wane
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:померкнуть.html>поме́ркла</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó sláva <b>pomérkla</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his fame dwindled</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pale <i>(before)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поместить.html>помести́ть</a> (5157)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мести́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместить.html>помести́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomestítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещать.html>помеща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to place, to put, to locate, to position, to set, to bestow, to stand</li>
<li>to invest</li>
<li>to lodge, to accommodate, to put up, to settle</li>
<li>to insert, to publish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поместиться.html>помести́ться</a> (13243)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместить.html>помести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li>to stay, to take a seat</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поместье.html>поме́стье</a> (12656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместье.html>поме́стье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poméstʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместье.html>поме́стья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместье.html>поме́стья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместье.html>поме́стий</a></b>)

***помесь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́месь</a> (21773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + a deverbal noun derived from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> ancestor of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месить.html>меси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mesítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to knead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (originally "to mix"). Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смесь.html>смесь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smesʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mixture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́месь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pómesʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́меси</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́меси</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помесь.html>по́месей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hybrid, crossbreed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mixture</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помеха.html>поме́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poméxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помеха.html>поме́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помеха.html>поме́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помеха.html>поме́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hindrance, barrier <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something which hinders</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<b>poméxoj</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You are very clever, cultivated, serious, you have immense talent, and perhaps a brilliant future awaits you, while I am an uninteresting girl of no importance, and you know very well that I should be only a <b>hindrance</b> in your life.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1940</b>,  Павел Петрович Бажов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pavel_Bazhov" class="extiw" title="w:Pavel Bazhov">Pavel Petrovich Bazhov</a>),  “Огневушка-Поскакушка  | The Dancing Fire Maid | ”, in  <cite>Морозко</cite>, Sverdlovsk |  translated as  “The Dancing Fire Maid”, in Eve Manning, transl., <cite>Malachite Casket: Tales from the Urals</cite>, Moscow, 195-, page 182:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сперва.html>сперва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круги́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ленькие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:потом.html>пото́м</a> бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> бо́льше, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сама́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подрастать.html>подраста́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ла</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:балаган.html>балага́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>пришёлся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помеха.html>поме́ха</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>Идёт</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:балаган.html>балага́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Spervá krugí málenʹkije davála, potóm bólʹše da bólʹše, i samá podrastátʹ stála. Balagán na putí prišólsja, tólʹko éto jej ne <b>poméxa</b>. Idjót, búdto balagána i net.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">First she made a small circle, then it got bigger and bigger and she began to grow too. The hut was in her way but it didn’t <b>hinder</b> her. She danced right through it as though it wasn’t there at all.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">First she made small circles, then bigger and bigger, and she herself began to grow. The hut got in her way, only it was no <b>obstacle</b> for her. She goes as if there is no hut.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1970</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>Наде́жда</a> Яковлевна Мандельштам (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nadezhda_Mandelstam" class="extiw" title="w:Nadezhda Mandelstam">Nadezhda Yakovlevna Mandelstam</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:германский.html>герма́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>посла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могло́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = ***помечтать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помечтать.html>помечта́ть</a> (23108)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечтать.html>мечта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mečtátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помечтать.html>помечта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomečtátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечтать.html>мечта́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dream for some time</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***помешательство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помешательство.html>помеша́тельство</a> (18899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ть</a>(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomešátʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешательство.html>помеша́тельство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomešátelʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешательство.html>помеша́тельства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешательство.html>помеша́тельства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешательство.html>помеша́тельств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>madness, insanity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> obsession, passion <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***помешать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ть</a> (2976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomešátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешать.html>меша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disturb, to hinder, to impede
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ть</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne éto móžet óčenʹ sílʹno <b>pomešátʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This can badly hinder me.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шнее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tebé ne <b>pomešálo</b> by sdélatʹ domášneje zadánije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It would be good if you did your homework.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помеха.html>поме́ха</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poméxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomešátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешивать.html>поме́шивать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешать.html>меша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> to stir; to mix, to mix up, to mingle, to blend, <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something for some time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забу́дь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помешать.html>помеша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:суп.html>суп</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne zabúdʹ <b>pomešátʹ</b> sup.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don't forget to stir the soup.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shuffle <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">playing cards</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***помешаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помешаться.html>помеша́ться</a> (23407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешаться.html>меша́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mešátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помешаться.html>помеша́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomešátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to go crazy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be obsessed with, to be a nut about <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помещать.html>помеща́ть</a> (15401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместить.html>помести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещать.html>помеща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomeščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместить.html>помести́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to place, to put, to locate, to position, to set, to bestow, to stand</li>
<li>to invest</li>
<li>to lodge, to accommodate, to put up, to settle</li>
<li>to insert, to publish</li></ol>

***помещаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помещаться.html>помеща́ться</a> (6057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещать.html>помеща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomeščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещаться.html>помеща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomeščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместиться.html>помести́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be (in a location), to be located <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">no perfective</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to fit</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещать.html>помеща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomeščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: to be housed, to be published</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ние</a> (1604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поместить.html>помести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomeščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lodgment, premise(s), room, apartment, quarters
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жилой.html>жило́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žilóje <b>pomeščénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">living quarters</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:караульный.html>карау́льное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">karaúlʹnoje <b>pomeščénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">guardhouse, watchhouse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́нии</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>pomeščénii</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">indoors</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрытый.html>закры́том</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́нии</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v zakrýtom <b>pomeščénii</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">indoors</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складской.html>складски́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ния</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skladskíje <b>pomeščénija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">storage facilities</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:безопасный.html>безопа́сное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bezopásnoje <b>pomeščénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">secure accommodation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>investment, location, placement</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помещичий.html>поме́щичий</a> (22222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещик.html>поме́щик</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poméščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помещичий.html>поме́щичий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poméščičij</span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> landowner</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> manor; manorial
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:помещичий.html>поме́щичий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poméščičij</b> dom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">manor house</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́н</a> (12297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomín</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́на</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>prayer for the dead, remembrance of the dead in prayer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>души́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">datʹ déneg na <b>pomín</b> duší</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">donate money for a diseased person to be mentioned in prayer</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>in expressions only</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">лёгок <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ljógok na pomíne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">talk of the devil</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помин.html>поми́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i v pomíne net</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is no trace/sign</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поминальный.html>помина́льный</a> (27496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pominátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́льный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-álʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминальный.html>помина́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pominálʹnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
